< review>
Best groomers in town. Would recommend for their customer service alone.

I work long hours and don't have much time during the day to schedule personal appointments, so when I got off work I called petco with plenty of time before closing to schedule a quick appointment for weeks away. After being told by a petco rep that someone was still in and could schedule an appointment for me i waited on hold for 30 mins. by the end of my 30 minute hold they closed shop and wouldn't schedule anything for me. that was the last time i went there.

After petco hung up on me, I called the dog spa and left a message. Less than 30 minutes later i get a text saying they can schedule my dog for an appointment the next day!!! They did that for me even after hours. From that point on I have been coming here. they do great haircuts and handle the animals really well.< /review>

<Review>I kept in mind that they are brand new and still in the process of hiring staff and smoothing out the kinks. The wait is a typical popular restaurant wait time for dinner hours. The waiter we had, Pierce, was wonderful. He made excellent recommendations and was attentive, considering the number of tables he was waiting on. < Review>
I really thought I'd like this new Mexican restaurant, but sadly I did not. We came during lunch hour (2pm).
The Margarita flight was the only thing my mom and I truly enjoyed.
I ordered a small Caesar Salad, one Fish Taco and one Chile Relleno and my mom ordered a 2 Combo Plate with a Carne Asada Taco and Shrimp Enchilada with a small bowl of Menudo.
The Caesar salad was delightful, the Chile Relleno was heavily battered and did not have much flavor. I ended up only eating the Chile. My mom said her shrimp enchilada was good but her taco wasn't anything special.
I never received my fish taco.
Our server was polite but seemed flustered, possibly due to understaffed FOH crew. Either way, when our food came out, they brought me the wrong dish entirely. Instead of a fish taco, they brought out a shrimp enchilada. Our server told us he would fix that. We both finished what they did bring out so I asked if he could just 86 the taco. He did and ended up gifting me a taco which was much appreciated. Unfortunately it was still not what I had originally asked for, but I couldn't be mad at a free taco.
In conclusion, I think I'll come back, but only for the margaritas and maybe a fish taco. I still want to try it.<//Review>

I wish they provided comment cards since they are currently doing a soft opening. I want to offer feedback solely in the hopes that they are able to use it to their benefit. Came here during the Grand Opening and this place was packed.

They have a lot of parking, but on a busy day you might have to park across the street.

As for the restaurant I would have to say it's the nicest and largest Mexican place in Temecula or Murrieta.  Has different wings with one a bar, outside eating, dining. Prices are beyond fair on meals and they have perfect portions.

Location is prime as its not far from the freeway exit and on the way to Pechanga.

Overall great place and will be back for sure.< /Review>

<Text>For a new Restaurant: Gewww!

Service: 1*
Food: 1*

Unreal! 45 minutes to receive our drinks and nearly 2hrs to receive our food. Unfortunately, we had to chase down our waitress for our check so that we could politely pay and finally leave!

< Text>
There was much hype surrounding the opening of this new Mexican restaurant so I decide to give it a shot.

At first look, the restaurant is beautifully built and the decor is very appealing.

We ordered a sangria sampler, the ceviche and an ice tea to start. The sangria sampler was watered down and about 80% ice. The tea tasted odd. Not sure if it is from a machine but it had an unappealing flavor. The ceviche was disappointing. The juice was red, but did not really taste like anything.

For our meal, we ordered enchiladas langosta and the fajitas (steak, chicken, and shrimp). The portions were generous. The enchiladas tasted good. Very flavorful. The beans and rice that accompanied it were acceptable.

The fajitas were a massive disappointment. The sizzling plate comes out and an entire restaurant watches as it is placed on a table. That was the most exciting part of this dish. It lacked flavor and was very bland. The veggies, the meats, the tortillas, the guacamole‚Ä¶.all could have benefitted by some simple seasonings. Specifically seasonings linked to Mexican dishes.

I wanted to love this place. It is a gorgeous setting, but the only thing authentically Mexican in this establishment are the paintings and names on the menu.</Text>

<user_name>F A</user_name>< Date>
1621567831991< /Date>
<rate>2<//rate>< review>
Soft Opening Review

First: The chips are beyond salty, I asked for new ones and she brought me a new bowl with warm but tiny end of the bag chips.

Second: If you plan to get ceviche go somewhere else, they call it ceviche but it is shrimp cocktail. It was pretty good but not what we wanted...since we thought we were getting ceviche.

Third: For fellow military families please be aware that their discount is only for the service member's plate. They told us it does not count towards the appetizer since he shared with the table. Therefore families with deployed service members (aka spouses) there is no discount for you or your children, they are only doing it as a courtesy for a service member that is present and on food he does not share even if he is the one paying the check. I have never known a restaurant to do it this way but just be informed on their policy.

Lastly, the young girl being trained was great! She was trying her best and had a positive attitude, the older lady training her seemed a little frustrated with the young girls mistakes which is unfortunate as the young girl was really trying! We liked her.

We won't be back. The food was okay but overpriced for the portions, most of it was really salty and lacked the authentic Mexican flavor. Also, the Dr. Pepper was flat so get water or try something other than soda.

Beautiful building with limited parking.< /review>

< Text>
We were told 45 min wait but waited ~80 mins. I'll attribute the wait to the crowd and typical new restaurant growing pains, it happens. That's fine. For me it was the long wait for our food once we were already seated and I really just didn't love the food. I had ceviche and tamales. I've had ceviche that was leaps and bounds better from grocery stores. The tamale filling was equivalent to frozen taquito filling and the sauce they served with it was a loose version of freezer bean and cheese burrito filling. I may have just ordered the two worst things on the menu because the rest of my family mostly liked everything. I will say that I LOVED the chips and salsa though. I dont think I would go back myself, only if someone invited me out and wanted to go there. I do think that the (mostly teenage) staff was doing their best and trying very hard. I liked every employee we came in contact with.<//Text>

< review>
This was the best experience I have had with a company in such a long time. Safelite on Wilson is top notch and they deserved to be recognized. I showed up for my 1PM appointment to get my Honda Civics windshield replaced. I was greeted by the person at the front desk whom went to get my technician Jordan. Jordan made a great first impression. He explained it would be around 2.5 hours due to my car having the ADAS camera and it having to be recalibrated after the windshield replacement. I waited in the shop (I had no ride üòû) while my car was being worked on. I felt very safe in the waiting area due to masks being mandatory and the chairs and such were 6 feet from each other. I worked on some homework and before I knew it Jordan came to grab me and said it was finished. I kid you not, it had only been just over an hour since he started on it. He explained the details such as what and what not to do in the next couple days to make sure the windshield sticks. He even stuck my parking permit sticker back on the new windshield. I am very pleased of the job that Jordan did. Jordan made the whole experience a breeze and I appreciate him very much. To everyone at safelite on Wilson I appreciate you and thank you for getting me in and out with such quality of work. Any management that reads this please tell Jordan he did an amazing job and I think he deserves a generous raise (or at least a bonus üòé)

- Matthew

< Text>
$5 Fridays!

Pavilions, owned by Vons, is a more upscale supermarket.  Fortunately, sale prices are good at both locations.

The layout is easy to decipher and the entirety of the store is kept clean and neat.  A pharmacy, deli, butcher, Starbucks and fresh sushi are on hand to make a one stop shop experience.

What brings me in are $5 Fridays.  From chicken wings to meatloaf, many a deal are to be had for just $5. Another enticement is clearance diving for any good finds I may spot.  Great for finding dinner!

Service has been good.  The deli employees are really great with gathering up what I need.  Parking is in a private lot, shared by Rite Aid and other businesses.

Pavilions is a great place to fulfill your grocery needs.  $5 Fridays are a great way to save & prices are competitive with other markets.

Recommend!<//Text>

< text>
A fully stocked grocery store with a pharmacy, bakery, florist, and deli.  There is also a Starbucks just inside the right-hand entrance so you can get your caffeine fix while you shop.

The manager of the bakery can be a bit brusque in how she speaks.  She is not quite rude but is also not entirely open and welcoming.  Their products are good but if a pleasant human interaction is important to your bakery experience you might wish to get your baked goods elsewhere.< /text>

My go-to store!

<Review>The employees are friendly here. I am not good about ad shopping or cutting coupons, so I can't honestly say how the prices compare, but I like a clean store that has all of my family's favorites. The convenience of having Rite Aid and Tuesday Morning in the same shopping center makes for one-stop shopping. The reason I don't do 5 stars is not the employees' faults, it's district offices that cut back on staff hours making it difficult to get anyone to help if you have a question or a return. In my days of working the grocery business, there was a customer service counter (that had someone always there) that helped with all of that. Now, you have to stand around waiting a long time for someone to come up and help you or you have to interrupt cashiers who are trying to help get lines down in the checkout lanes. Not good for customer service.</Review><pics>None< /pics>< Resp>

<Review>It's funny writing a review for a grocery store... it's so everyday and common that I didn't think it needed a review. But like restaurants and other service industries, the people need to know what to expect when they glide past the sliding doors! Since this is a Pavillions (an extra posh version of a Safeway or Vons), it includes a Starbucks, a full bakery, a full deli, a full butcher, a full florist, and a sushi chef! It's got everything! The cashiers are all really friendly and they always have plenty of courtesy clerks available to help find anything. It's a big store so they have a lot of options on the shelves that the smaller stores don't have. VERY large alcohol selection.</Review>< rate>
